līlayā netre karābhyāṃ pidadhe sa tenābhūttrilocanaḥ  Bhmj tṛtīyanayanodbhūtavahninā so bhavadgiriḥ pluṣyatsālalatājālajvālāvalayitāmbaraḥ  Bhmj tato gaurīgirā cakre punargaurīguruṃ girim smerapuṣpalatāvṛkṣaṃ dṛśā śītāṃśuśekharaḥ  Bhmj tatra pṛṣṭo bahuvidhāḥ kathāḥ praṇayalālasaḥ devyā kathānte bhagavānūce dharmārthanirṇayam  Bhmj pravṛttānāṃ sadācāraṃ varṇāśramavibhāgajam nivṛttānāṃ ca niḥsaṅgakriyānirvāṇajaṃ phalam  Bhmj tataḥ śaśāṅkacūḍena pṛṣṭā devī mṛgīdṛśām śaśaṃsa puṇyaṃ caritaṃ varārādhanadaivatam  Bhmj athābravīnnīlakaṇṭhaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ sarvairmunīśvaraiḥ kāraṇaṃ paramaṃ viṣṇuṃ bhūtānāṃ prabhavāpyaye  Bhmj vasudevasya tanayo bhaviṣyati hariḥ kṣitau aṃśāvatīrṇo vibudhārātisaṃhāratatparaḥ  Bhmj sa sūryaḥ sa ca śītāṃśu so haṃ sa ca caturmukhaḥ sarvadevamayaḥ śauriḥ kaṃsakeśiniṣūdanaḥ umāpaterapi puraḥ śrutamasmābhirīśvarāt  Bhmj etacchrutvā munivaco dvārakāmetya keśavaḥ avāpa putraṃ rukmiṇyāṃ svecchāsṛṣṭajagattrayaḥ  Bhmj dhanyo si yasya te rājankamalāvallabho vibhuḥ viśvarakṣāmaṇiḥ so yaṃ goptā garuḍalāñchanaḥ  Bhmj  umāmaheśvarasaṃvādaḥ    kathayitveti gāṅgeye muhūrtaṃ maunamāsthite ūce munisabhāmadhye śanakairdharmanandanaḥ  Bhmj daivataṃ paramaṃ śarma kimekaṃ sarvadehinām kasminpratiṣṭhitaṃ viśvaṃ stutyā muktipradaśca kaḥ  Bhmj ityukte dharmaputreṇa babhāṣe jāhnavīsutaḥ manasā puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ natvā viṣṇumanāmayam  Bhmj ananto bhagavānviṣṇurdevadevo jagatprabhuḥ stuto nāmasahasreṇa mokṣado garuḍadhvajaḥ  Bhmj jagatpratiṣṭhitaṃ tasmindaivataṃ paramaṃ ca saḥ nāmnāṃ sahasraṃ munayo yasya gāyanti muktaye  Bhmj viśvaṃ viṣṇurvaṣaṭkāro bhūtabhavyabhavātmanaḥ prabhorbhūtabhṛto bhūtabhāvanasya bhavacchidaḥ  Bhmj patyuḥ puṃsaḥ purāṇasya kṣetratretrajñasākṣiṇaḥ bhuvaḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ śaṃbhorvidhāturvedhaso vidheḥ  Bhmj harerhiraṇyagarbhasya śrīpatorviśvakarmaṇaḥ vṛṣākaperamoghasya sahasrākṣasya gopateḥ  Bhmj sahasraśiraso viṣṇorvyāpinaḥ praṇavātmanaḥ stotraṃ nāmasahasrāṅkaṃ mantrarājaṃ pracakṣate  Bhmj ityuktvā vaidikairdivyairgauṇamukhyaiśca nāmabhiḥ sahasrasaṃkhyaistuṣṭāva deva bhīṣmaḥ sanātanam  Bhmj śrutvaitatprayataḥ kṛṣṇaṃ vanditvā dharmanandanaḥ prabhāvaṃ bhūmidevānāṃ papraccha dyunadīsutam  Bhmj so vadadbrahmaniṣṭhānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ bhayātkila udeti somaḥ sūryaśca prayāti ca samīraṇaḥ  Bhmj dattātreyavarāvāptasahasrabhujamunmadam kārtavīryaṃ purā prāha vāyurjitagattrayam  Bhmj brāhmaṇebhyaḥ paro nāsti rājendra balavattaraḥ bhavādṛśā dṛśā yeṣāṃ bhavanti na bhavanti ca  Bhmj somaputryā vṛtaḥ pūrvamuttasthe yādasāṃ prabhum tatkāmamapibatkopāddayitāmājahāra ca  Bhmj nirjitākhilagīrvāṇagandharvā dānavāḥ purā sṛṣṭo triṇā śītakaraḥ śakraṃ ca cyavano jayat  Bhmj surāṇāṃ daityasamare rakṣitā timire purā sṛṣṭo triṇā śītakaraḥ śakraṃ ca cyavano jayat  Bhmj iti brāhmaṇamāhātmyaṃ śrutvā haihayabhūpatiḥ arjuno pujayannityaṃ bhūmidevānānanyadhīḥ  Bhmj  pavanārjunasaṃvādaḥ    ataḥ paraṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ prabhāvaṃ keśavo vibhuḥ jānāti nābhinalinasvecchāsṛṣṭacaturmukhaḥ  Bhmj iti bhīṣmeṇa kathite hṛṣīkeśaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ papraccha vipramāhātmyaṃ sa ca pṛṣṭastamabhyadhāt  Bhmj purāhaṃ raukmiṇeyena pṛṣṭaḥ śaktiṃ dvijanmanām avadaṃ tapasā yeṣāṃ kampante daivatānyapi  Bhmj putra sarvaprayatnena pūjaya brāhmaṇānsadā ete krodhaprasādābhyāṃ jīvayanti dahanti ca  Bhmj pratiśrāyarthī durvāsāḥ purā dīptākṣimūrdhajaḥ uvāsa madgṛhe taistaiḥ sevyamānaḥ priyairmayā  Bhmj sa bhuktvā pāyasaṃ taptamucchiṣṭena ruṣā jvalan limpāṅgānīti māmāha taccāsmyakaravaṃ bhayāt  Bhmj rukmiṇīṃ sa rathe kṛtvā babhrāma bahuyojanam nirvikāraṃ ca māṃ dṛṣṭāva tutoṣa paruṣāśrayaḥ  Bhmj sa māmūce tavocchiṣṭaliptaṃ vajramayaṃ vapuḥ bhaviṣyati vinā pādau tau niliptau yatastvayā  Bhmj  durvāsaso bhikṣā    etatkṛṣṇavacaḥ śrutvā pārthaḥ śāntanavātpunaḥ śuśrāva devarājarṣivaṃśānkalmaṣanāśanān  Bhmj kaṇvairabhyavakrītavasiṣṭhabhṛgukaśyapān duḥṣyantarāmanahuṣālarkaśvetabhagīrathān  Bhmj kathayitvā kṣaṇaṃ sthitvā tūṣṇīṃ niḥśabdasa puraṃ vyāsājñayā pārthaṃ visasarja suravrataḥ  Bhmj kṛṣṇena saha kaunteyo bhrātṛbhiśca sahānugaiḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ puraskṛtya prayayau hastināpuram  Bhmj pūjyamānaḥ surairdātā sthitvā tatra yudhiṣṭhiraḥ dṛṣṭvottaraṃ sa saṃprāptaṃ punarāyātpitāmaham  Bhmj sānugaḥ sa samabhyetya gāṅgeyaṃ śaraśāyinam praṇamya pāṇḍavo smīti nigadya samupāviśat  Bhmj munīndrajuṣṭe sadasi brahmaloka ivāpare jāte niḥśabdasaṃcāre bhīṣmavaktrāvalokini  Bhmj śanairunmīlya nayane pāṇḍavānvīkṣya sānugān vāggamī gambhīramavadadgāṅgeyaḥ pāṇḍavāgrajam  Bhmj kāle diṣṭyā bhavānprāptaḥ parivṛtte divākaraḥ māsadvayamatītaṃ me niśātaśaraśāyinaḥ tvāmāmantrya vrajāmyeṣa putra lokānsanātanān  Bhmj ityuktvā satyadugdhābdhiḥ kiṃcidāvṛttakaṃdharaḥ uvāca vidurasyāgre dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ pitāmahaḥ  Bhmj rājanvidyāmayaṃ cakṣurakṣuṇṇāṃ tava lakṣyate mā gamaḥ putraśokārtyā mohaṃ kālo hi durjayaḥ  Bhmj putravatpaśya bhūpālamanṛśaṃsaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram prayātu śeṣaḥ kāle yaṃ tava saṃtoṣaśālinaḥ  Bhmj etaduktvā hṛṣīkeśaṃ stutvā mūrdhnā praṇamya ca babhāṣe bhagavangantumanujānīhi māmiti  Bhmj atha kṛṣṇābhyanujñāto nistaraṅga ivodadhiḥ muhūrtamabhavadbhīṣmo dadhānaḥ prāṇadhāraṇām  Bhmj antaḥ sparśarasāttasya gātrāṇi tyajato bahiḥ viśalyāni śanaiḥ sarve dadṛśurvismayākulāḥ  Bhmj sa galitasakalāntaḥsvāntaviśrāntimūlodgatanijabalaśaktisphoṭitāśeṣacakram vitatataralatārasphāratejaḥprakāraprasṛtamarududañcanmadhyanāḍikrameṇa  Bhmj lalitadalasarojaproccaṭajjīvahaṃso dṛśamatiśaśisūryāṃ bhrūvibhāge niveśya galitakaraṇavṛttigrāmaniḥsyanādalakṣyaḥ sapadi kimapi bhīṣmaścintayansaṃbabhūva  Bhmj  bhīṣmotkrāntiḥ    atha jyotistaḍitpuñjarāṃśuśatācitam bhittvā bhīṣmasya mūrdhānaṃ viveśa vimalaṃ nabhaḥ  Bhmj tato sya ratnābharaṇairvāsobhiḥ kusumaistathā dharmarājaḥ saviduraścakre vaimānikaṃ svayam  Bhmj chettraṃ tasya yaśaḥ śubhraṃ yuyutsustūrṇamagrahīt cāmare sattvadhavale bhīmasenārjunāvapi  Bhmj sabāṣpaṃ bharatastrībhistālavṛntānilena saḥ vījyamānaścitāṃ prāpa śrīkhaṇḍāgurukalpitām  Bhmj sajīva iva saṃlīne gāṅgeye sphāratejasi yudhiṣṭhiramukhāścakruḥ sāśrunetrā jalakriyām  Bhmj tatra mandākinītīre viṣaṇṇo rājñi sānuge jalamadhyātsamuttasthau jāhnavī sāśrulocanā  Bhmj sā vihvalā śokavatī viṣaṇṇaiḥ paramarṣibhiḥ vyāsanāradakaṇvādyairmuhurālokitāvadat  Bhmj hā putra tripurārātiśiṣyasya kṣatriyadviṣaḥ jetā tasyāpi rāmasya nihato si kathaṃ paraiḥ  Bhmj aho nu tvayi kālena yāte staṃ yaśasāṃ nidhau śocyeyaṃ pṛthivī śūnyā vīraratnavinā kṛtā  Bhmj kā nāma jananī pāpā madvidhānyā bhaviṣyati nihataṃ tvādṛśaṃ putraṃ yā śrutvāpi na dīryate  Bhmj aho bata varākeṇa hato bhīṣmaḥ śikhaṇḍinā kupitaḥ kuñjarārātirjambukena nipātitaḥ  Bhmj iti pralāpamukharāṃ jahnukanyāṃ janārdanaḥ śanairāśvāsayannūce meghagambhīraniḥsvanaḥ  Bhmj vijñātaparamārthāpi vasuśāpe pi sākṣiṇī sāmānyajananīva tvaṃ kathaṃ devi vimuhyase  Bhmj na hi śāntanavaṃ bhīṣmaṃ tripurāriparākramam hantuṃ śikhaṇḍinaḥ śaktirvinā kālādbalīyasaḥ  Bhmj sa yātaḥ paramaṃ dhāma svacchandanidhanaḥ svayam aśocyaṃ mā śucaḥ putraṃ ko nyo jāyeta tadvidhaḥ  Bhmj iti vyāsādibhiḥ sārdhaṃ kṛṣṇenāśvāsitā śanaiḥ niḥsyandamīnamakarā kṣaṇaṃ mandākinī babhau  Bhmj tato yudhiṣṭhiramukhāstāṃ samāmantrya sānugāḥ duḥkhākulā nyavartanta yāte staṃ vāsareśvare  Bhmj iti śāntiparvaṇi dānadharmāḥ samāptāḥsamāptaṃ śāntiparva
